# mapping
# ng/ñ -> r
# oe/ö -> l
# eo/ö -> l
# yu/ü -> v
# aa/ā -> q
# gw/ģ -> x
# kw/ķ -> z
# j/y  -> j

# keyboard layout
# ā w e ñ t y   u i o p
# a s d f g h/ö z k l
# ķ ģ c ü b n   m
